[30;1m73 | [0m[35m<p>The IDLE extension allows an IMAP server to notify a client when something[0m
[30;1m74 | [0m[35mchanges in a mailbox. It can be used as an alternative to polling to receive[0m
[30;1m75 | [0m[35mnew messages.</p>[0m

[30;1m78 | [0m[35msomething happens in the selected mailbox until the client ends the IDLE mode[0m
